    background: transparent !important;

    text-shadow: none !important;
  }

    text-decoration: underline;
  }

    content: " (" attr(href) ")";

    content: " (" attr(title) ")";

  a[href^="javascript:"]:after {
    content: "";
  }

    border: 1px solid #999;
    page-break-inside: avoid;
  }
  thead {
    display: table-header-group;
  }

    page-break-inside: avoid;
  }

  }

    orphans: 3;

  }

    display: none;
